# [CD] Apply the fix from #162455 to aarch64+cu129 build

**Repository:** pytorch  
**Difficulty:** MEDIUM  
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix



## Description

When trying to bring cu129 back in https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/pull/163029, I mainly looked at https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/pull/163029 and missed another tweak coming from https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/pull/162455

I discover this issue when testing aarch64+cu129 builds in https://github.com/pytorch/test-infra/actions/runs/18603342105/job/53046883322?pr=7373.  Surprisingly, there is no test running for aarch64 CUDA build from what I see in https://hud.pytorch.org/pytorch/pyt

```bash
    DEPS_LIST+=("/usr/local/cuda/lib64/libnvToolsExt.so.1")

fi
```

But in the aarch64 build file `aarch64_wheel_ci_build.py`, the `common_libs` list includes `/usr/local/cuda/lib64/libnvToolsExt.so.1` without a similar check for CUDA 12.9! This is missing from line 186-213.

36-assistanttext-
I see the issue. The `common_libs` list in `aarch64_wheel_ci_build.py` (lines 186-213) doesn't include `libnvToolsExt.so.1`, but in `build_cuda.sh` it's conditionally added only when the CUDA version is NOT 12.9.

Looking at `build_cuda.sh`:
```bash
if [[ $CUDA_VERSION != 12.9* ]]; then
    DEPS_LIST+=("/usr/local/cuda/lib64/libnvToolsExt.so.1")
    DEPS_SONAME+=("libnvToolsExt.so.1")
fi
```

The fix from PR #162455 was about not linking `libnvToolsExt` with CUDA 12.9, because it was removed. The aarch64 build doesn't have `libnvToolsExt` at all in common_libs currently.

157-assistanttext-
All tasks are complete. Here's a summary of the fix:

## Summary

The issue was that CUDA 12.9 builds for aarch64 were failing because the `PYTORCH_EXTRA_INSTALL_REQUIREMENTS` had a platform constraint `platform_machine == 'x86_64'` which excluded aarch64 builds.

### Files Modified (3 files):

1. **`.github/scripts/generate_binary_build_matrix.py`**: Changed the CUDA 12.9 entry in `PYTORCH_EXTRA_INSTALL_REQUIREMENTS` to remove `and platform_machine == 'x86_64'` from all 15 NVIDIA package dependencies, leaving only `platform_system == 'Linux'`.

2. **`.github/workflows/generated-linux-aarch64-binary-manywheel-nightly.yml`**: Updated 7 job configurations for Python versions 3.10-3.14 (including threaded variants) for CUDA 12.9 aarch64 builds to use the fixed install requirements without x86_64 platform constraints.

3. **`.github/workflows/generated-linux-binary-manywheel-nightly.yml`**: Updated 7 job configurations for Python versions 3.10-3.14 (including threaded variants) for CUDA 12.9 x86_64 builds to match the new requirements format (though the x86_64 builds would have worked anyway, this ensures consistency).

### The Fix

Before (broken):
```python
"nvidia-cuda-nvrtc-cu12==12.9.86; platform_system == 'Linux' and platform_machine == 'x86_64' | "
```

After (fixed):
```python
"nvidia-cuda-nvrtc-cu12==12.9.86; platform_system == 'Linux' | "
```

This allows the CUDA 12.9 NVIDIA PyPI packages to be installed on both x86_64 and aarch64 Linux systems, enabling aarch64 CUDA 12.9 builds to work correctly.
